                        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);\n                            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);\n         function getElementsByClass(searchClass,node,tag)\n                    {\n                        var classElements = new Array();\n                        if ( node == null )\n                                node = document;\n                        if ( tag == null )\n                                tag = '*';\n                        var els = node.getElementsByTagName(tag);\n if (transitionTarget.size() == 0) {\n                            toggleTarget.toggleClass(toggleCssClass);\n                            return;\n                        }\n                        var fromHeight, toHeight;\n\n                        transitionTarget.height('auto');\n                        fromHeight = transitionTarget.height();\n                        toggleTarget.toggleClass(toggleCssClass);\n                        toHeight = transitionTarget.height();\n\n                        // check whether transition is supported\n                        transitionTarget.css(transitionStyle);\n                        if (!(transitionTarget.get(0).style['transition'] || transitionTarget.get(0).style['WebkitTransition'])) {\n transitionTarget.height(fromHeight);\n\n                        if (toHeight < fromHeight) {\n                            scrollAnimate(toggleTarget, 800);\n\n                            toggleTarget.toggleClass(toggleCssClass);\n                            transitionTarget.one('transitionend',function(){\n                                transitionTarget.removeAttr('style');\n                                toggleTarget.toggleClass(toggleCssClass);\n                            });\n                        }\n                        else {\n                            transitionTarget.one('transitionend',function(){\n                                transitionTarget.removeAttr('style');\n                            });\n                        }\n\n
